Page 9

Current Affairs Commentary

Taking Over Shanhaiguan and the Far Eastern Situation Shu 40

Since the fall of Linyu on January 1st of last year, followed by the ravaging of Rehe and the threat to Tianjin and Beijing, the entire China was almost completely detached from its peacetime state. When the Tanggu Truce was established, this disguised war between China and Japan came to a halt. However, the disturbances in Luandong and the repeated connivance of the Japanese army, coupled with our country's inability to directly suppress them, have caused the people of Luandong to fall into double suffering. Looking eastward in anticipation, one cannot help but feel grief and indignation. Recently, Japan's diplomatic policy has undergone technical changes, hence the more lenient expression. Therefore, there have been negotiations for the return of the passes of the Great Wall, and it is also rumored that Linyu, the first pass in the world, will be returned on the 10th of this month. Before this takeover, we must learn from our past pain and offer our opinions so that our countrymen can have a renewed understanding and a more in-depth assessment of the current international situation, especially the Far Eastern situation.

First. We must recognize that the return of Shanhaiguan this time is not because the Japanese have awakened and want to fundamentally reconcile with China and voluntarily return it. It is merely a change in diplomatic policy. On the one hand, it aims to ease the momentary anger of our people, and on the other hand, to relax the temporarily tense international situation. Moreover, the area east of Tianjin is full of bandits and thorns. If we do not work hard to govern, it will provide the enemy with a pretext and make us a laughingstock in the international community. If we promote the virtuous and the capable and earnestly reorganize, we will be hindered everywhere and invite future disputes. The difficulty in handling China's diplomatic problems has not yet ended.

Second. We must know that the loss of our country's territory in the past two years or so is far more than just Luandong, and even more than just the Shanhaiguan Pass. The loss of over 4.2 million square miles of land and over 30 million people is being endured with patience and humiliation. If Linyu can indeed be returned as scheduled, our people should not think that this is enough, but should work even harder to find a way to revitalize ourselves.

Third. We must know that since the September 18th Incident, the powers, apart from providing moral assistance through spiritual sympathy, have no other real means. China cannot use force to recover what was lost, nor can it easily defend its borders. China's situation is already very dangerous. Now, the powers are engaged in an economic struggle against Japan, which is very intense. The Japanese also know that their natural resources, industrial organization, and military quality all have shortcomings that are not easy to remedy. Therefore, they have drastically changed their diplomatic policy and temporarily adopted a policy of conservation and development. However, this economic struggle will eventually become a military struggle. At this time, it is impossible for China to maintain peace through arms, and it is difficult to remain strictly neutral. Even joining any side is not allowed by the circumstances. Therefore, we should take advantage of the fact that the situation is not yet settled and the countries are not yet fully prepared to make a thorough assessment and find a good way to strengthen ourselves.

In addition to the above three points, we must further make a detailed analysis of the world situation and have a concrete observation of the Far East. Now, Japan does not dare to engage in military adventures again, but instead seeks to maintain its gains and ensure that its so-called "Japan-Manchuria controlled economy" can be gradually realized. This way, it can ensure its supply of coal and iron, become self-sufficient in agricultural products, and have room for maneuver with the United States and the Soviet Union. The plan to wage war in other countries' territories is still a superior strategy. This is the old trick of the Russo-Japanese War of 1904. As for the struggle between Britain and Japan and between the United States and Japan, it is all about the exclusive control of markets. In the short term, the United States may not cross the Pacific to take military offensive measures, and Japan has no ambition to seize the Americas. If relations between China and Japan can be eased slightly, Japan's convenience in developing Eastern markets will be far greater than that of the United States. Britain's current situation is also only to maintain the status quo of its existing interests, so that the so-called economic alliance within the empire can be firmly established and overcome the centrifugal tendencies of its various autonomous territories and colonies. Then, its naval vanguard base, Hong Kong, will definitely have a reliable guarantee due to the construction of the Singapore naval base. The special rights of the Far Eastern market will also not decline. We should assess the Far Eastern situation and look at the overall situation in the Pacific Ocean, and we should immediately issue a profound introspection. It is absolutely inappropriate to repeat the mistakes of the past. Moreover, the return of Shanhaiguan may not be a sign of awakening on the part of others, but we should make a painful and silent recognition. The lessons of Goujian's restoration of his state should ultimately be an ancient mirror for the Chinese people.

Yan Huiqing Arrives in Beijing to Meet Lin and Wang 41

To Go to Tianjin This Morning and Return South in Half a Month

Statements Made in Beijing

(Nanjing) Yan Huiqing and Yan Deqing arrived in Beijing by train at 9:00 am on the 5th from Shanghai. Vice Minister Xu Mo and dozens of Foreign Ministry officials greeted them and went directly to official residence No. 7 on the railway to rest. Then, they met with Chairman Lin and President Wang. Wang hosted a banquet for Yan in the evening. Yan is scheduled to go to Tianjin on the morning of the 6th and return to Beijing and Shanghai in half a month. According to Yan, he has been abroad for two years, from Washington to Geneva to Moscow, and may have a gap in his understanding of the domestic situation. Diplomacy is backed by the government and public opinion. Without knowing the government's policy and understanding the trend of public opinion, it is impossible to take measures. The current international situation is extremely urgent, but there will not be drastic changes in four or five months. Therefore, he is returning to the country to ask the government for instructions and to handle personal matters. He will return to Russia in three months at the earliest or half a year at the latest. During this trip to Europe, European countries were quite skeptical of China, but they are still quietly observing our future attitude. The puppet regime is brewing to become emperor, and the countries will definitely not recognize it. Russia is indeed fully prepared for war, but does not want to provoke it. Other countries also hold the same attitude. Our country is currently in an extremely dangerous period, but it is not without a way out. Geneva is one way, Moscow is one way, and Tokyo is also one way, but all should be prepared to overcome difficulties with great determination, so as not to be controlled by others. Not only the government has this preparation, but the whole country must also work together to achieve success. (5th dispatch from Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) Yan Huiqing said that Ge Gongzhen is still in Russia and has traveled extensively in the Russian states. He is very interested in this kind of life and is currently writing a book about the Russian social situation. (5th dispatch from Central News Agency)

British Nationals Unauthorized Mining on Yunnan Border 42

China Will Lodge a Protest

(Nanjing) The central government has received a telegram from the Yunnan Provincial Government reporting that British nationals have been mining in the undetermined Nongbang area south of Pianma on the border of the province without obtaining the consent of the Chinese government, which is an infringement of sovereignty. It is reported that the Political Council will order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a protest with the British ambassador to stop it. (5th dispatch)

Russia and Japan Step Up War Preparations

British Newspaper Publishes Secret Japanese Plan to Attack Russia

Russia and Japan Order Large Quantities of Steel and Iron in the United States (Washington) According to a representative of a major steel factory speaking to reporters, Russia plans to order steel and iron worth millions of dollars in the United States. Recently, Russia has inquired about all prices from more than 1,600 steel factories in the United States, mostly regarding steel pipes and steel rails for oil mining and other materials for transportation, in preparation for a war with Japan. The National Trade Bank, which is being planned by President and Director-General of the Financial Relief Bureau Jones, may accept this credit loan. However, there is a reciprocal trade agreement between the United States and Russia, and Russia will also import a large number of export goods into the United States, so very little cash is needed for trade between the two countries. According to a report from the US Department of Commerce, US exports to Russia in December of last year were $570,269, compared to only $186,310 the previous year.

Russian imports into the United States in December of last year totaled $1,071,550, an increase of $552,817 compared to the previous year. Russia has been vigorously purchasing steel and iron materials in recent years in preparation for a Russo-Japanese war, while Japan is also actively preparing. Last year, Japan ordered a not small amount of steel and iron in the United States, totaling 592,536 tons, an increase of 401,343 tons compared to the previous year. According to the US, last year's total steel and iron exports were 1,350,692 tons, with total national exports of $1,675,020,000, with cotton exports accounting for the largest share at $398,212,263. (4th dispatch from National News Agency)

(London) The Daily News today published an article by Cummings entitled "Japanese War Plan," accompanied by a detailed map of Japanese marching traffic in northern Manchuria. According to reports, the map was obtained from a high-ranking official, has never been published, and the powers are not fully aware of it. The map shows that Japan plans to build a railway from Qiqihar to Sakhalin, and a military road from Harbin to Lahasusu, bypassing the side of the proposed Jiagou (transliteration) to Ningguta and Lahasusu railway. It also plans to build a railway from Solun to Hailar, so that there will be a double line directly to Manzhouli. The article also states that aircraft fields have been built in Hailar, Mogen (transliteration), Sakhalin, Manzhouli, Ningguta, Mishan, Suifenhe, and other locations along the Soviet-Russian border, and a military highway of 7,360 kilometers is currently under construction. (5th dispatch from Reuters)

Japanese Newspapers Report This

The Pravda commented on this, saying, "If the news reported by the Nichi Nichi Shimbun is true, then this repeatedly proves that the British imperialist's aid to Japanese imperialism is not only not weakening, but is increasing day by day. The British people's open aid to Japan's invasion of Manchuria, the clear and unambiguous statement they have made, is that Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations does not lose its right to rule the trust islands in the Pacific, and the desire to express its invisible loan policy through the method of not taking opposing Japanese dumping, etc., is a mark of this policy, and the conclusion of the gentleman's agreement is a completion of this policy. British imperialism is directing the main direction of its foreign policy towards competition with the United States, and is organizing anti-Soviet Union actions, while at the same time retaining its alliance with Japan by all means. The gentleman's agreement that is currently being transmitted is the condensation point of this alliance." (4th dispatch from TASS)

Singapore's Anxiety 44

Residents Prepare for Air Defense Singapore's recent news is complex, and the naval conference may have a far-reaching impact on our future. Local newspapers have been paying close attention to Ellen B's whereabouts. Some say that he has changed his plans and gone to Java from other places, and others say that he is attending the naval conference. The average person is in the dark about what is being discussed, and those who have experienced the last war especially hope not to see war again. However, it is universally acknowledged that we cannot sit here and wait for death. Many houses in our coastal recreation area have been taken over by the military, and our beautiful airport will soon be used for monsters such as tanks to practice. As for the situation in the air, what is known is that in the recent joint exercise of the naval and air forces, one plane crashed. The reason is said to be that the fog was so thick that they could not see each other. The residents are all anxious about how to avoid air raids and how to dig bomb shelters. The only solution is to dig tunnels in all our small hills. (January 20th, Singapore correspondence from the North China Daily News)

Hirota's Policy Toward Russia First Resolve Outstanding Issues 46

Conclusion of a Non-Aggression Treaty

Still Uncertain

(Tokyo) In this afternoon's Budget General Assembly, after questions and answers between Seiyukai's Kiyose Kikuo and Navy Minister Osumi regarding naval issues, he questioned the Foreign Minister, saying, "Japan's credibility seems to be causing considerable misunderstandings in the world. What will the authorities do?"

Hirota replied, "If the people's beliefs are firm, then misunderstandings will naturally be swept away. The government should, of course, make every effort to make people recognize the true Japan. Therefore, efforts have not been relaxed in this regard." Kiyose then asked, "Since the rejection of the non-aggression treaty, how should the authorities deal with the changes in Japanese-Soviet relations?" The Foreign Minister replied, "Japan has not yet rejected the non-aggression treaty and intends to study it in detail in order to deal with it. The Soviet Union has continuously wanted to find ways to resolve the problems between the two countries. Japan has long held the policy of first resolving outstanding issues and then contacting the non-aggression treaty. I think that if the outstanding issues are resolved, then it may not be impossible to conclude the treaty." Then, Mr. Washino reiterated the theory of respecting the people and pressed the Minister of Commerce and Industry. There were many more questioners. Because today was the last day of the Budget General Assembly, the intensity of the debate was extraordinary. The meeting adjourned at over 6:00 pm, which was past the scheduled time. (5th dispatch from the Japan Union News Agency)

First Russian Ship in Seventeen Years Arrives at a US Seaport 47

Carrying Salt to Vladivostok for Gas Production

San Francisco For nearly seventeen years, not a single ship flying the Soviet Russian flag has sailed into a Pacific US port. Today, the Russian cargo ship Kalis arrived here, which the public found very strange. Hundreds of people gathered on the waterfront to watch. The ship has now loaded salt and is sailing to Vladivostok, reportedly for use in Siberian fishing grounds. However, according to San Francisco newspapers, this salt can be used to produce a type of gas. This is the fifth batch of salt shipped to Vladivostok. The previous batches were all transported by American ships. (4th dispatch from National News Agency)

Gold Price Depreciation Makes US Finances Abundant 48

Treasury Balance of One Trillion Dollars

(Washington) The US government's budget needs to be in deficit by $2,000,000,000, but today the Finance Department said that since the dollar was devalued to fifty-nine cents and six mills, there can now be a surplus of one trillion dollars. According to the statement, after the dollar depreciation, the government profited $2,805,512,061, so the cash balance in the treasury at the end of January was $4,064,781, and on February 1, it changed to $7,018,263,781. The $2,000,000,000 in the Stable Exchange Fund was drawn from this account. (4th dispatch from National News Agency)

US, UK, and French Currency Stabilization Issues 49

Currently, There Is No Basis for Formal Discussion

Roosevelt Decides to Further Devalue the Gold Dollar 50

(London) A report from Washington states that the Treasury Department suddenly announced that the equalization fund has not yet been established, temporarily alleviating concerns that the United States will use this fund to instigate a currency war. It is rumored that the United States has not sought opinions from London or Paris regarding currency stabilization issues. According to general opinion, there is no basis for formal discussion until the dollar has reached its correct standard price and its value has been reduced. However, President Roosevelt is still determined to further devalue the dollar. Reuters' New York dispatch states that Mr. Gannett, who recently visited the White House, is confident that the price of gold must continue to rise, as the current price only prevents prices from falling. The Brookings Institution in the United States, the highest authority on American economic and financial matters, also expressed its opinion through its currency expert, Mr. Pasvolsky, that prices have only risen by 20%, while the price of gold has already risen by 60%. The amount of gold flowing into the United States from England recently is still limited, which is only due to shipping companies being unwilling to transfer large quantities of private gold and fast ships not sailing frequently. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

(London) Today's London gold price is 140 shillings, 5 shillings higher than the French franc exchange rate, but about 2 shillings lower than the New York price. Therefore, the price difference between Paris and New York is over 7 shillings. This is why £1,540,000 worth of gold was sold in London, and a large amount of cash was transferred to New York. Although a lot of cash is being transferred to the United States, the dollar has shown no signs of weakness. It is expected that this trend of the dollar will continue as gold can be continuously shipped out in Europe. This is because the return of funds has just begun, and European investment in New York securities is booming. In addition to this temporary reason, the United States has a continuing favorable trade balance, which may encourage gold to flow to New York in the future. The purpose of American policy is to increase export trade, but it is unwilling to receive foreign goods to offset the price of American goods, nor is it willing to retain surplus funds abroad. Therefore, all parties believe that the time is not yet ripe for the British authorities to stabilize the pound sterling. The Financial News stated that banks believe that the suspension of the gold standard by France and other gold-using countries is a matter of time, and some criticize France's policy of maintaining its un-conservative position, resulting in the consumption of gold reserves. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Balkan Pact Established 51

United Opposition to Revising Treaties

Bulgaria Still Needs to be Brought On Board

Belgrade – The four major Balkan countries have now completed a united front to oppose Italy's proposal to revise the Treaty of Versailles. These four countries are Greece, Turkey, Romania, and Yugoslavia. Their main purpose is economic and political cooperation, with a particular emphasis on united opposition to the revision of the Treaty of Versailles. The foreign ministers of the four countries have held multiple meetings within 48 hours and have today signed the agreement they have negotiated. Although the full text of the agreement has not been published, it is reliably reported that the above points are its outline. This agreement guarantees peace between the signatory countries, so it is generally referred to as the Locarno Pact of the Balkans. However, Bulgaria, which is currently the cornerstone of the Balkans, has not yet joined, so the agreement cannot yet be regarded as complete. The signatory countries are now making every effort to persuade Bulgaria to join, but the other party has not yet expressed its approval. Bulgaria currently insists on several requirements as conditions for joining the agreement. These requirements are: (1) Bulgarian minorities in neighboring countries should enjoy freedom of education, religion, and language; (2) equality in armaments; (3) land access to the Aegean Sea, claiming that this was promised by the Treaty of Neuilly. Greece has resolutely refused to allow Bulgaria to have this corridor, believing that this would cause Greece to lose its richest tobacco-producing province. It was initially feared that Yugoslavia would not want to offend Bulgaria and might not sign the agreement, but it has now also joined. King Alexander of Yugoslavia is more politically astute than most monarchs and is expected to strongly urge King Boris of Bulgaria to join the agreement. Although no one expects all of Bulgaria's demands to be acknowledged, it is hoped that a compromise can be reached. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Prudent Expectations for Bulgaria's Accession 52

Past Mistakes are Like Yesterday's Death

Belgrade – A communiqué was issued here, stating that the foreign ministers of Greece, Romania, Turkey, and Yugoslavia have initialed the final and definitive clauses of the Balkan Peninsula Agreement and have decided to hold a formal signing ceremony in Athens this week. The full text of the agreement will be published immediately after the signing. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

Athens – The Balkan countries' agreement was initialed yesterday in the Yugoslavian capital. Prime Minister Tsaldaris made the following statement to the press regarding this matter: (The Balkan countries' agreement safeguards the borders of each contracting state and does not oppose any country. Its conclusion is indeed a major event. The establishment of this agreement not only guarantees peace in the Balkans but also allows countries to trust each other, which benefits general peace. This agreement establishes the foundation for close and proper cooperation in the Balkan Peninsula, which is greatly beneficial to the development of economic and other interests. I firmly believe that all nations that desire peace will warmly welcome this agreement, and not long after, other Balkan countries such as Bulgaria and Albania will also be able to join together.) (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Belgrade – The Balkan Peninsula Agreement, which was initialed this afternoon, has a validity period of five years. The communiqué issued a moment ago did not indicate the contents of this agreement. Political circles explained the reason for the silence, saying that this agreement still needs to be submitted to Bulgaria for its accession. For the sake of prudence towards Bulgaria, its contents are not being disclosed. The "Political Newspaper" recently wrote an article on the Balkan Pact, proposing a slogan: (The Balkans are for the Balkan people.) It also stated that the ideal of national unity, which is unacceptable to most nations in Europe, has now begun to be realized in the Balkan Peninsula. Europe already has a (Western Locarno Pact,) and now it is supplemented by an (Eastern Locarno Pact.) The various past mistakes and faults of the Balkan countries are like yesterday's death. Romania, Yugoslavia, Greece, and Turkey are ready to move towards the path of tranquility and security. What will be Bulgaria's attitude? Will it continue to wallow in the scope of foreign conspiracies? If Bulgaria still holds a wait-and-see attitude and wants to take risks and chances as in the past, then it is indeed a big mistake. After the four countries in the Balkan Peninsula are united, they will surely make such adventurous attempts impossible to succeed. Conversely, if Bulgaria joins the agreement, it can join the rest of the countries in working for peace in the Balkan Peninsula. As far as we ourselves are concerned (referring to Yugoslavia), we must do everything we can to ensure the implementation of the second method, because only Bulgaria's accession to the agreement is Bulgaria's only turning point. Moreover, the results of the Balkan Entente will soon have an impact on European politics. The Balkan Peninsula has always been a volcano in Europe, but it will not be so in the future. As far as Turkey is concerned, its territory in Europe has been secured, so it can concentrate on seeking the consolidation of its own country. Although former Greek Prime Minister Venizelos is no longer in his position, his policies have indeed been implemented. Its territorial integrity has been secured, and its domestic political situation has also been stabilized. As for Romania, the former great politician Xanasca and his disciple, the current Foreign Minister Titulescu, have always strongly advocated the Balkan Pact. Now that their proposals have been realized, they can also be proud of themselves. As for our country (referring to Yugoslavia), we have become a strong fortress for the independence of the Balkan countries and the most solid guarantee for Balkan peace. This is our glory.) (Havas dispatch, 4th)

Ankara – The Turkish government has decided to hire a French financial expert to be responsible for studying Turkey's financial situation and drafting a report on reforming Turkish finances. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Anxious Atmosphere at the Meeting of the Chamber of Deputies

(Paris) The atmosphere in Paris is very tense. The Parisian defense forces have been ordered to remain in their camps, as have the suburban defense forces, to prevent accidents. Since the discovery of the Bayonne fraud case, Paris has been the center of an uproar, especially today. The government's mobilization of troops to prevent disturbances during tomorrow's debate has aroused the anger of the opposition. According to a right-wing organ, tanks are currently being driven out of the Compiègne military camp, and two detachments of troops have been ordered to go to Paris. In addition, the troops stationed in the Paris area have received instructions to prepare for an emergency, as it is rumored that the royalists are planning to launch a demonstration. Tomorrow's debate in the Chamber will be very intense, but since the Socialist Party has decided to support the government because of the dismissal of Police Chief Chiappe, the Daladier government can be temporarily preserved, and those who support Daladier also welcome his skills in dealing with difficult situations. Paris Police Chief Dismissed

Prime Minister Declares a Thorough Investigation of the Fraud Case

With the support of the Socialist Party, Prime Minister Daladier may not fail in the debate in the Chamber of Deputies on Tuesday. The reorganization of the cabinet, such as Marchandeau as Minister of Finance and Penancet as Minister of War, are all results of Mr. Chiappe's dismissal. However, although the Daladier government has the support of the Socialist Party, its lifespan is still uncertain. Whether it can support itself for two months like the Chautemps government is still uncertain. Mr. Cipo, the Governor of the Seine Province, has now replaced Mr. Chiappe as the Paris Police Chief and took office this morning, immediately engaging in maintaining public order in Paris. Daladier declared that he is determined to thoroughly investigate the Bayonne fraud case to find out the truth, which has slightly consolidated his position. Daladier claimed that he did not want to participate in the debate on this case as reported in the newspapers, but wanted to order the investigation committee to proceed as soon as possible after the Congress meeting. Hitler's Centralization of Power Completed 69

Has the Power to Appoint and Dismiss Federal Officials

Conflict with Göring Not Resolved

(Berlin) The authorities issued several special orders, the most important of which is that the President granted the power to appoint and dismiss Prussian officials to Prime Minister Hitler. The power to appoint and dismiss officials in the remaining federal states belongs to the respective federal civil affairs chiefs. In the future, the President still has the power to pardon soldiers convicted by military courts, etc., but the power to pardon other cases belongs to Prime Minister Hitler. (National Telegram, 4th)

(Berlin) Germany's move to reduce the powers of the fourteen federal states and three cities has now been completed. The German Reform Act, which stipulates the reduction of the powers of the federal states, was promulgated today after being signed by President Hindenburg. According to this law, Prime Minister Hitler has the power to appoint and dismiss Prussian officials and has the power of pardon. This approach may lead to a conflict between Hitler and Prussian Prime Minister General Göring. The two leaders often disagree on some important matters, such as the church dispute. Göring advocates radicalism, while Hitler advocates mediation. Previously, the power to appoint and dismiss Prussian officials belonged to Göring, but now this power has been transferred to Hitler. General Göring will surely express his dissatisfaction. Prussia is the largest state in Germany, with a population of 37,000,000 and an area of 113,740 square miles, with Berlin as its capital. Hitler can appoint and dismiss officials in Prussia in accordance with the new law, but the powers of dismissal, appointment, and pardon in other states are delegated to the civil affairs chiefs of the National Socialist Party. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Zhu Shaoliang Organizes Three Support Ningxia Columns 87

= Song Zheyuan and others come forward to mediate =

= Sun's army's three-phase plan for advancing westward =

Beijing Correspondence: Sun Dianying's army is pressing on Ningxia's provincial capital and has been in a stalemate with Ma's army near the city for days. Sun's troops occasionally attack the city, resulting in repeated battles. Ningxia Chairman Ma Hongkui sent a telegram to Beijing on the morning of the 2nd, reporting that the enemy troops were stubbornly resisting at Zhujiazai and Beita north of the city and that elite troops have been dispatched to actively suppress them. Ma also urgently telegraphed Deng Baoshan, Commander-in-Chief of the Left Wing, to order Lu Dachang's troops from Ningxia and Shuofang to suppress the enemy. After receiving the telegram, Deng returned from Xi'an to Lanzhou to arrange military affairs. According to a telegram from Lanzhou, the three provinces of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai have mobilized six divisions, awaiting orders from the Central Government to attack Sun's army. Zhu Shaoliang also organized three support Ningxia columns to advance in different directions to support Ningxia, with Lu Dachang, Yang Qu, and Deng Baoshan serving as commanders. According to a military source, Sun Dianying has established a Ningxia Provincial Government in Dengkou. Lu Fengnian's troops stationed in Baotou have crossed Wuyuan westward to reinforce the front. Because Sun's army suffered too many casualties in the attack on Ningxia, part of the army detoured towards Ningxia and Shuofang in an attempt to cut off the connection between the Gansu and Ningxia armies. Furthermore, the 86th Division stationed in northern Shaanxi and Yue Xiu's troops have been ordered to mobilize and prepare to attack the flanks of Sun's army near Li Gangbao. Jing Shiyuan, originally stationed in Yulin County, dispatched the 258th Brigade to Hengshan, Fugu, and Shenmu Counties after receiving the order. The 125th Brigade was stationed in Bao'an Anzhai and other areas, jointly defending with Lu Dachang's troops from Gansu, under the command of Zhu Shaoliang. Xu Tingyao's troops have also been ordered to prepare to go to Suiyuan to monitor the reorganization of Sun's troops. Wang Jingguo will command his troops to block Sun's troops. If Sun Dianying still refuses to accept the reorganization, a major war in the Northwest may be unavoidable. Ma Hongkui sent a telegram to Kang Shishu, the representative stationed in Shanxi, to explain the true situation of the military at the front. It is said that Sun Dianying, having failed to capture Ningxia after a long siege, and lacking supplies and transportation in the rear, is in a dilemma. He recently sent two telegrams to Zhang Guanwu, who had previously been mediating, asking him to intercede with He Yingqin, willing to comply with the order to withdraw, and requesting that senior officials be sent to supervise. After receiving the telegram, Zhang telegraphed Sun from Tianjin, advising him to comply with He Yingqin's order to withdraw troops on the 30th, and saying that even if he managed to capture Ningxia temporarily, how could it last long? Zhang arrived in Beijing last night to meet He, who said that if Sun's army did not comply with the order, the only option was to take the final measures. As for Sun's request to send senior officials to supervise the withdrawal of troops, the Military Council has sent senior staff officer Men Bingyue to Suiyuan. If Sun wants to negotiate, he can discuss with Men nearby without the need to send other senior officials. Zhang Guanwu, who has old friendships with both Sun and Ma, has decided to mediate for peace, hoping for an early end to the war. Song Zheyuan is very concerned about this and has also decided to come forward to mediate, ordering his representatives to discuss with the representatives of both parties stationed in Beijing. Therefore, Zhang Jianhou invited Wang Shiping and Bai Jianmin, the representatives of Sun and Ma stationed in Beijing, and Song's representative, to discuss with Zhang Guanwu and others. He also telegraphed Hu Jiesan in Tianjin to come to Beijing to meet at a certain place tonight (the 3rd) to discuss the first step of the plan. After the principles are agreed upon, they will proceed separately. Hu Jiesan is scheduled to come to Beijing tonight. Han Fuqu, Chairman of Shandong, is also concerned about the war between Sun and Ma and recently sent Liu Xizhong to Beijing, which is related to the peace movement. According to those who came to Beijing from Baotou today (the 3rd), the troops fighting with Ma's troops on the front line in Ningxia are commanded by Ding Futing and Liu Yueting of Sun's army, totaling more than 30,000 people. Sun Dianying is commanding military affairs in Dengkou. The war news received in Baotou said that on the 28th of last month, Sun's army had captured the new Ningxia city. Ningxia originally had two cities, new and old. The new city is seven or eight miles west of the old city. Ma Hongkui's and Ma Hongbin's troops, numbering about 20,000, are defending the old city and confronting Sun's army. Zhu Shaoliang telegraphed Sun's plan to invade the west, saying that, according to Ma Bufang's telegram (dated the 24th), a table of Sun's army's operational plans was seized and is forwarded as follows: (1) The main point of the first phase of the offensive is to first occupy Shizuizi, making it easier for our large army to advance in different directions and take advantage of the victory to go south, avoiding our army's delay in the wilderness. (2) The main point of the second phase of the offensive is the city of Pingluo County. In addition to the cavalry following the plan to cut off the enemy's reinforcements, our army should advance in two directions, with the central route directly attacking the Great Wall, and the left and right wings should use encirclement tactics, first cutting off their reinforcements to discourage them, making it easier for the central route to succeed. Second, attacking Ningxia will cause Pingluo to fall without being surrounded. All our senior commanders must break through Ningxia in the shortest possible time. Cavalry Commander Yu Shiming and Forward Commanders Yang Yaofeng and Gao Xiaxuan should follow the plan, send competent staff officers to search for enemy information, and report at any time. (3) The main point of the third phase should be to use all our strength to defeat the enemy's cavalry and advance to Guangwuzhen and Zhongwei, in order to directly attack Gansu and find a way to capture the rebel Ma Hongkui alive. Our army's plan, though clearly three, is actually one. All our generals must judge clearly and achieve a concerted effect. (3rd)

Honolulu, the Paradise of Aviation (Honolulu Correspondence) 88

There are no storms, no sudden heat, and no severe cold here. It is the most peaceful and mild place in the Pacific Ocean. Spring is here all year round, and flowers bloom everywhere. This is the Hawaiian Islands, made up of twenty islands. This is a mountainous place and also volcanic. The natives who live here have not yet shed the barbarism inherited from the past. The total population, including pure natives and mixed-race people, is only about 60,000. Politically, it is nominally ruled by the United States. The governor and officials of various departments are selected by the President of the United States. However, Americans number only 45,000, including expatriate Americans. But there is a phenomenon that makes Americans uneasy and fearful, that is, the number of Japanese immigrants increases every year. There are now almost 140,000 Japanese, ranking first among all the people in Hawaii. Although our Chinese compatriots in Hawaii number only 30,000, they are all very wealthy and have a considerable economic advantage. However, in recent years, affected by the decline of the sugar industry, the overall economic situation is not as good as before. The military facilities here were originally centered on Pearl Harbor. There were originally only 1,600 soldiers and 100 officers, with the aim of maintaining American transportation in the Pacific and preserving the right to navigate the Panama Canal. Coastal batteries and airfields were set up in Pearl Harbor and other important areas, and six barracks were built. Recently, due to the stimulation of Japan's expansion of armaments, especially after the Mukden Incident, Japan not only occupied Manchuria but also wanted to include North China, and even dominate the Pacific. At this time, the United States is, of course, very worried, so it transferred the Atlantic fleet to the Pacific to prepare for any eventuality. Therefore, it is necessary to build a large-scale military port in Pearl Harbor and Honolulu, making this place the base of the United States Navy and Air Force in the Pacific. As a result, the docks have been enlarged, oil storage tanks have been built, and continued expansion is planned, with the aim of giving it the military strength to control the Pacific. However, according to what I have heard here, Japan's military expansion is truly unprecedented in its scale and speed. Americans are naturally very fearful of this, especially Japan's so-called Second Replenishment Naval Plan, which is even more alarming. Before this plan was completed, Japan's auxiliary naval vessels were already much stronger than those of the United States. After this plan is completed, the United States will be at a greater disadvantage. What is the value of the slight superiority of a few capital ships? Moreover, Japan also wants to expand eight air squadrons, which is not enough to threaten Pearl Harbor, but the Philippines and Guam are very dangerous. Therefore, the American naval and political circles believe that a crisis is imminent and that there should be vigilance. Therefore, some people, including Swenson, advocate that the United States should expand its navy and not believe in the current superiority of American capital ships. In particular, the communication of the air squadrons in the Pacific is even more important, because at this moment, or in the near future, the American Navy has no possibility of taking an offensive against Japan, and even a favorable defensive posture is not very reliable. Therefore, in today's situation, the only way to develop aviation and try long-distance flights can create new significance in military affairs. The United States Navy transferred six elite P2 and Y1 type bomber aircraft, organized into a long-range flight team, led by Major McKinnis as the commander of the flight team. The team departed from San Francisco at 0:00 PM (Pacific Standard Time) on January 10 and was discovered outside Honolulu at 0:19 PM on the 11th. At 0:49 PM, it landed in Pearl Harbor, covering a total distance of 2,089 nautical miles and taking a total of 24 hours and 49 minutes. Flying from the base of the U.S. Pacific Navy, San Francisco, to the advanced naval base in the Pacific, Pearl Harbor, in one day and night is a major event in the Pacific and the first act in the competition between the United States and Japan. From this non-stop flight and 15-hour night flight, we have two of the most important understandings: First, the United States will pay more serious attention to changes in the Pacific in the future. If the flight connection between Pearl Harbor and Manila is successful, the problem will become more serious. Second, the role of the Navy will take a back seat, and the competition between the United States and Japan will focus on the Air Force in the future. (January 11, 1934)

The Seventh Route of the Eastern Route Bandit Suppression Army is Organized 89

= Will be trained along the Yangtze River in Anhui Province =

= Fujian Provincial Militia Ordered to be Disbanded =

Xiamen Correspondence: After the 19th Route Army withdrew from Quanzhou on January 25, they first gathered in Hui'an, and then went to Putian, Fuqing, and Xianyou to gather separately. Jiang Dingwen, Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Route Front, received a telegram from Chairman Chiang, ordering the 19th Route Army to be reorganized into the Seventh Route of the Eastern Route Bandit Suppression Army, with Mao Weisui as the Commander-in-Chief and Zhang Yan as the Deputy Commander-in-Chief. Mao and Zhang immediately telegraphed from the Hui'an army headquarters on the 30th to take office. The original telegram stated, "Having received the appointment certificate No. 1294 from the Nanchang Headquarters of the Military Commission of the National Government, I hereby appoint Mao Weisui as the Commander-in-Chief of the Seventh Route of the Eastern Route Army, etc. I have respectfully taken office at the Hui'an defense headquarters on January 30. Weisui et al. are mindful of the ongoing national crisis and pledge to continue to fight with the past spirit of resisting Japan and suppressing communism, to stop disputes and defend against insults, to support the Central Government, to be united in mind and virtue, and to implement from beginning to end. I hope that you will give us guidance from time to time to correct our shortcomings. In addition to submitting reports and issuing orders separately, I respectfully report, Mao Weisui, Commander-in-Chief of the Seventh Route of the Eastern Route Army, and Deputy Commander-in-Chief Zhang Yan." After the telegram was sent, the name of the 19th Route Army was immediately canceled. The Seventh Route was organized into four divisions, abolishing brigades, with three regiments per division, and still using the numbers 49, 60, 61, and 78 for the four divisions. Each division has jurisdiction over three regiments, and the commanders above the regimental level are all reassigned by the Central Government. At the same time, the Military Commission announced the appointment of Wu Chengren as the commander of the 49th Division, Chen Pei as the commander of the 60th Division, Yang Tingya as the commander of the 61st Division, and Wen Chaoji as the commander of the 78th Division. Chen Pei was transferred from his current position as the commander of the 28th Brigade of the 10th Division. Wu Chengren is from Pucheng, Fujian, and was transferred from his current position as the deputy commander of the 36th Division and commander of the 106th Brigade. Wen Chaoji is from Guangdong and was transferred from his current position as the chief of staff of the 83rd Division. Yang Tingya was transferred from his current position as the deputy commander of the 3rd Division. All are generals who have contributed to this entry into Fujian. The positions below the division commander will be filled after the completion of the counting. Jiang Dingwen sent Zhao Nan, chief of staff of the Northern Route Front Headquarters, to Quanzhou by air on the 30th to make arrangements. After Mao and Zhang telegraphed to take office, Zhao flew back to the province. At the same time, Jiang telegraphed Xiamen, ordering Zhang Jiong, adjutant of the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters, to lead a group of adjutants and a platoon of guards to Quanzhou on the 31st to count each unit. Once the counting is completed, the four divisions will be organized according to the organization, and the regimental commanders of each division will then take office. As for the rumors that a part of the troops will be transferred to western Fujian to suppress bandits, it is not reliable. It is only heard that after the four divisions are organized, they will be trained along the Yangtze River in Anhui Province.

Since the 19th Route Army has been completely resolved, in the Longyan area, there is only one regiment of infantry led by Zhou Lixing, who withdrew from Zhangzhou, and one battalion of artillery from the 78th Division, and 600-700 students from the officers' training school, for a total of only 2,600-2,700 people. Together with Xu Minghong's volunteer army, there are no more than 4,000 people. The Central Army has only advanced to Longyan since the 3rd Division recovered Zhangzhou. Therefore, the remaining troops of the 19th Route Army, which retreated to Longyan, can still defend Longyan without leaving. Xu Minghong and Cai Tingkai are also still in Longyan. As for the rumors that the Guangdong army led by Huang Renhuan occupied Longyan, they are also inaccurate. Except for small detachments from each of Huang Renhuan's and Huang Yanzhen's divisions still stationed in Wuping and Shanghang, there are no Guangdong troops entering Yongding, Pinghe, and Zhao'an on the border between Fujian and Guangdong. Also, on the afternoon of January 29, three Guangdong planes flew from Shantou to reconnaissance over Zhangzhou, Pinghe, Zhao'an, and Xiamen, but have not been seen again. As for the Central Army in Zhangzhou, there are only about two regiments, about 3,000-4,000 people, from the 3rd Division, and no large forces. In addition, there are militias and punitive armies everywhere. According to yesterday's (1st) news, a part of the 83rd Division of the Central Army will come to Xiamen from Quanzhou by three ships, Xinfeng, Kunxing, and Taishun, and go to Zhangzhou and then to Longyan. It is heard that they will continue to suppress bandits in western Fujian. Also, the military affairs of Fujian have been completely resolved after the reorganization of the 19th Route Army and the inauguration of Mao and Zhang. From now on, it will move from a military period to a post-war period. Militias in various places will be disbanded in turn. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek telegraphed to militias in various places on the 30th of last month, ordering them to concentrate on the spot and await reorganization and not to move without authorization. Therefore, Du Qiyun, Yang Fengnian, Lin Zhiyuan, Song Yuanyuan, Xu Ruilin, and others arrived in the province on the 1st to meet with Jiang Dingwen. It is heard that they are all discussing the post-war problems of the militia. (February 2nd)

｜The Pure Bandit Area Has Shrunk Invisibly｜

Nanchang Correspondence: Military News, since the Red Bandits have been gradually pushed forward by the National Army's Three Guarantees policy, the pure bandit area in Jiangxi has shrunk invisibly. Now only Ningdu, Ruijin, and Shicheng counties remain. Gao'an News, at 8:00 PM last night, the 60th Bao of the 1st District was patrolling when three porters suddenly passed by on the road within the sentry line. The sentries Yao Fengxiang and Zhang Qinsheng saw them and immediately issued a password. The porters, upon hearing the sound, abandoned their burdens and fled. The sentries immediately intercepted their burdens. Upon inspection, it was found that there were three loads of salt. They immediately reported to the Bao chief. Upon receiving the news, the Bao chief immediately sent militiamen to track and arrest them. The three salt carriers were captured. It is heard that they and two loads of salt have been escorted to the county government for interrogation. February 3rd

Post-Disaster Yellow River Project Fundraising Methods 91

Proposed Jointly by Five Provinces to the Central Government for Handling; Jinan Correspondence: Last year, the Yellow River breached in three places, resulting in an unprecedented catastrophe. Although the breaches at Lanfeng and Xiaopangzhuang have been closed, the breach at Shitouzhuan on the north bank remains unresolved. With the arrival of freezing temperatures and the accumulation of ice, the project is increasingly difficult to manage, and the disaster remains severe. The embankments along both banks of the river have been washed away, collapsed, and damaged, even more so than before. In the future, if another flood occurs, the consequences would be unimaginable. Recognizing this, the Yellow River Conservancy Commission previously formulated three fundraising methods for post-disaster projects and telegraphed them to the relevant five provincial governments of Henan, Hebei, Jiangsu, Anhui, and Shandong, seeking unanimous approval and requesting the Central Government to allocate funds for construction. The three methods are as follows: (1) Implement surcharges on railways, postal services, and steamships, following the previous Yellow River breach handling methods; (2) Have the relevant provincial governments designate appropriate guarantees, such as local taxes, to issue Yellow River breach closure and post-disaster project bonds; (3) Request the National Economic Council to allocate a certain amount of cotton and wheat loans as subsidies. The authority for the first and second items rests with the Central Government. Regarding the second method, the Shandong Provincial Government has made thorough plans and, after deliberation by the Political Affairs Conference, telegraphed its approval. Other provinces have also unanimously approved. It is reported that a joint request has been submitted to the Central Government for approval. Today (the 3rd), the Provincial Government has instructed the Shandong River Affairs Bureau regarding the case. The original order stated: (The document from the Yellow River Conservancy Commission states that the Yellow River overflowed last year, causing damage to several provinces, and the loss of life and property is incalculable. Currently, the embankments on both banks have been washed away, collapsed, and damaged, even more so than before. If post-disaster repairs are not carried out urgently, then with the imminent arrival of the flood season, not to mention encountering another flood, the collapse and overflow could inundate Wei in the north, potentially affecting Tianjin and Tanggu, and seize Huai in the south, potentially harming Jiangsu and Anhui. The devastation would be unimaginable. Even if a normal water level is encountered, the residents along the river will inevitably suffer many hardships. The Commission, responsible for river management, looks ahead with great anxiety. It has dispatched personnel separately to assess the post-disaster projects, but construction has not yet begun due to financial difficulties. The current situation is urgent and cannot be delayed any longer. Three fundraising methods are proposed: (1) Implement surcharges on railways, postal services, and steamships, following the previous Yellow River breach handling methods; (2) Have the relevant provincial governments designate appropriate guarantees, such as local taxes, to issue Yellow River breach closure and post-disaster project bonds; (3) Request the National Economic Council to allocate a certain amount of cotton and wheat loans as subsidies. Although the above two methods may inevitably increase the burden on local people, it is necessary for preventing disasters, protecting people's lives and property. It is proposed that the Commission, in conjunction with your government, the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, and the governments of Henan, Hebei, Jiangsu, and Anhui provinces, jointly telegraph the Central Government for approval. If you agree, please reply by telegram so that we can proceed. Commissioner Kong Xiangrong has been dispatched to make contact and send separate telegrams. This telegram is sent for your information. We previously telegraphed that (items 1 and 2 can be handled as proposed, the authority rests with the Central Government, please take the lead in drafting a joint telegram, and the second item, which requires local guarantees for the issuance of bonds, will be submitted after careful planning.) Subsequently, the Secretariat of the Provincial Government forwarded a telegram from Commissioner Kong Xiangrong, and the 294th Political Affairs Conference resolved to (reply by telegram with approval). In addition to replying by telegram and distributing it separately, Commissioner Kong Xiangrong's telegram is copied and sent to the Bureau for its information. This order.) (3rd)

Shandong Library Theft Case: Court Begins Investigation 92

｜Principal Offender Si Zhengmin Changes Testimony｜Jinan Correspondence: Si Zhengmin, the suspect in the theft of antiques from the Shandong Provincial Library, was transferred from the Military Law Office to the Shandong Higher Court for handling yesterday, as reported previously. After accepting the case, the Shandong Higher Court determined that it should be handled by the Procuratorate of the First Instance District Court and returned the case to that office the day before yesterday. Prosecutor Zhu Weiran of the District Procuratorate accepted the case for handling. Yesterday (the 2nd), Prosecutor Zhu began the first investigation in the Second Investigation Court of the District Procuratorate. First, he ordered the bailiffs to bring the suspects Si Zhengmin and his wife from the detention center. He questioned Si Zhengmin about the process of stealing the antiques. After Si Zhengmin stated his place of origin, age, and occupation, he said that on January 21, at dawn, he (Si referring to himself) went to Daming Lake to skate. He noticed a person standing alone by the riverbank, with his eyes fixed on him. He became suspicious and left the lake. The person saw him move and ran to the base of a tree not far away. At this time, he saw that two people were already squatting under the tree. As he approached, they dispersed. When he reached the tree, he saw two straw bags placed by the river, as well as five porcelain plates that were not wrapped. There was also a small boat in the river. He recognized the items as those displayed in the library and thought they had been stolen. He initially intended to return them to the library, but feared being accused of theft. He then placed the straw bags on the boat and hid the porcelain plates at the bottom of the lake. He used the small boat to transport the items to the west side of the Li Gong Temple, so that he could take them home and store them temporarily. After only one day, he feared that the porcelain plates in the water would be stolen or damaged, so he went to retrieve them on the 23rd of this month and was arrested. He was repeatedly interrogated by the Public Security Bureau and transferred to the Military Law Office. He had to give the previous account of the situation under severe interrogation. Given the size of the missing items, it was impossible for him to steal them alone. He unfortunately found them and was arrested. He has no way to defend himself. The three thieves were strangers to him, and he does not know their names. Since the thieves cannot be arrested, he cannot escape responsibility. He hopes to be treated leniently when sentenced. He is extremely grateful, and so on. The prosecutor then said, "Your statement is clearly an attempt to evade responsibility. The testimony is self-contradictory. Who are you trying to blame? You said yourself that you could not have done this alone, and people believe that one person could not have done this. But they cannot believe that there was no one else involved in the theft," and so on. The prosecutor then questioned Si's wife, Zhao. After questioning for about three hours, they were dismissed from the court. Si Zhengmin and his wife were returned to detention to await further investigation. (3rd)

Songjiang: Two Suspects Arrested in Xinzhuang Robbery Case 93

Seven robbers armed with weapons suddenly broke into the home of Liu Guanfu, a villager in Xinzhuang 39th District, at the end of last month and robbed him. The local Fifth Police Station was notified to investigate. After investigation by detective Qu Liansheng, it was discovered that a local resident, Xu Yisheng, pawned items at the Huichang Pawnshop in Xujiahui, Shanghai, and tore up three pawn tickets and threw them on the ground as he left. Deeming this suspicious, Qu returned to Xin on the 2nd. At around 9 PM that night, he saw Xu Yisheng lying in a horizontal position in a smoking den in the town. He took Xu back to the station for investigation. Xu confessed immediately and admitted his guilt. He also implicated his accomplice, Tan Baoxing, who had also been present at the robbery. Tan was also subsequently arrested. A written confession was recorded, and they were escorted to Songjiang for legal proceedings today (the 5th).

Female Corpse Discovered at Jiaochang in North City 94

A female corpse was found in a pond in the Zuoying Jiaochang (military training ground) inside the North Gate of the city. The face of the corpse was submerged in the pond, making it unidentifiable. She was wearing a dark blue cotton coat, and a cane was discarded nearby. She was about forty years old. The area is very quiet. It is unknown why the woman took her own life or if she was murdered. The local police have reported the matter to the prosecutor's office for investigation. So far, no family members have come to the scene to identify the body.

Qingpu: Accountant Robbed En Route 95

Chu Yiming, a rice merchant from Xiema Bridge, Kunshan, was robbed on his way back to his store from collecting accounts in the city at around 8 PM the day before yesterday. He was attacked with a club and injured on the head at Bazhi Bridge, about three miles from the Xiaoxi Gate. He lost consciousness and did not wake up until 3 AM yesterday. Upon checking his belongings, he found that he had been robbed of over 100 silver dollars, an account book, and a watch.

Jiashan: Robbers Posing as Passengers Rob Merchant Ship 96

A cargo ship departing from Zhongdai Town in the southern part of the county for Jiaxing has been operating for many years and has a good reputation. Therefore, many shops load and unload goods on it every day. On the morning of the day before yesterday, the ship was fully loaded with goods and over a dozen passengers. As it approached the Shibali Bridge area, a strong young man jumped up from the ship and pulled out a gun, ordering the ship to stop. At the same time, five men wearing short clothes searched the cabin. After the robbery, they all headed towards the car road. By the time the Shibali Bridge security team received the news and gave chase, the robbers had already fled far away. The total loss is estimated at over 560 yuan. The case has been reported to the county for investigation.

Jiaxing: Yuxian Town Robbery Case 97

At around 9 PM on the 3rd, two thugs suddenly entered Shen Baocheng's Nanhang goods store in Yuxian Town, Jiaxing, south of the Gangnan Guangsheng Bridge. After entering, they closed the door and ordered silence, claiming to borrow 200 yuan. The partners, seeing the situation, did not resist and allowed them to open the account box. They robbed all the 272 silver dollars and several hundred dimes. After the two robbers left, the Sixth Public Security Bureau of the town was notified. Bureau Chief Zheng Hui went to the scene for inspection and ordered the police to pursue the robbers, but their whereabouts are unknown.

Water Police Captain Inspects He 98

Liu Zuhan, the captain of the First Water Police Brigade, considered the security of the inland rivers during the winter months to be of great importance. He departed from the province the day before yesterday to inspect the defense in the Jiahu area. He has now completed inspections in Linghu, Nanxun, Jiashan, Pinghu, and other places. On the 5th, he arrived in He from Pinghu. At 11 AM, the Fifth Squad of this area went to the port to greet him. After arriving at the port, Captain Liu went to the squad headquarters. In the afternoon, he departed to inspect the defense and review the water police. He then went to Wangdian for inspection before returning to the province.

Wuxi: Chief Prosecutor Succession 99

Zhou Erkai, the Chief Prosecutor of the Wuxi County Court, was transferred to the regular post of Prosecutor at the Wuhu District Court in Anhui Province by order of the Ministry. His vacancy was filled by Qian Chengjun, the former presiding judge of the Criminal Division of the Shanghai District Court. Qian arrived in Wuxi the day before yesterday and discussed the transfer issues with Chief Prosecutor Zhou. Yesterday (the 5th), the new and old prosecutors officially took over. After the handover, Zhou will take a 20-day vacation as usual and plans to travel to Beijing first. He is expected to assume his new post in Wuhu after the Lunar New Year.

The Silk Industry Amidst the Tragic Decline of the Silk Market 100

The silk factory industry in Wuxi has suffered significant losses due to the tragic decline of the silk market and sluggish foreign sales. Most factories have ceased production. Only twelve companies, including Huaxin, Yongtai, and Ganxing, are struggling to remain open, accounting for only a quarter of the industry at its peak. Their situation is also precarious. Recently, the Silk Industry Control Council will soon be established in Hangzhou, and silk sales in Europe and America have gradually improved as various silk factories resume work. The Shanghai, Zhejiang, and Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Association recently held a meeting in Shanghai to discuss ways to rescue Chinese silk. It has been approved by the Economic Commission to allocate 2 million yuan from the American wheat loan for the rescue of the silk industry after the establishment of the Silk Industry Control Council. Therefore, silk factories in Shanghai are preparing to resume production. However, the factories in Wuxi that have already stopped production must wait until the silkworm season this spring for the silk market to improve before there is any hope of recovery.

Tragic News of Two Elderly Women Burned to Death 101

At 3 AM yesterday (the 5th), a fire suddenly broke out at the home of Xie Benda and Xie Erda on Xie Lane, Guangqin Road, outside the North Gate. Fire brigades from various sections rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire, but it was too late. All the houses were reduced to ashes. Xie's mother, Ms. Xie, over sixty years old, was unable to escape and perished in the flames. It was truly tragic. In addition, in the 15th District of the county, in Tang Xijing's grandmother's house in Qianzhou Town, Xianwubang, at night, after sleeping, Ms. Tang, over eighty years old, overturned the foot warmer in the bed, which burned the bedding. She could not be rescued in time and was burned to death by the fire. Fortunately, the fire was quickly extinguished, and the house was saved.

Romantic Woman Commits Suicide After Love Affair Gone Sour 102

On the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, a modern woman, named Chen Qiyun, arrived at the Wuxi Hotel near the Gongyun Bridge. She wore a bluish-gray coat with a black leather collar, a black brocade crepe camel hair qipao, and a white cotton short shirt inside. She was beautiful, about twenty years old, and could speak Mandarin, Shanghainese, and Suzhounese. She booked Room 33 and then moved to Room 28. She acted generously. Until the night before last, five men visited the woman one after another and talked intimately until late at night before leaving. At around 1 PM yesterday, three more men went to visit her. The tea boy opened the door and entered, only to find Chen moaning on the bed, pale. The tea boy knew something was wrong and immediately took her to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. It was determined that she had ingested raw opium. Treatment was immediately administered, and she was fortunate to survive. According to Chen, she was originally from Peiping but moved to Shanghai at a young age. Her father was a judge at the Shanghai District Court and is now deceased. She attempted suicide because of a failed love affair. At around 10 PM that evening, Lu Fengqi, Zhou Ruquan, Gu Huai, and others visited the hospital. They moved Chen from the hospital to Deng Xiangsheng's residence in Yingshanhe in the city. Their actions were very mysterious.

Changzhou: Appeals After Tax Increase on Kerosene 103

The Wuyi Manufacturing Machinery Industry Association, reporting that the new tax on kerosene has been implemented, requires an additional 25 yuan in customs duties per ton of diesel fuel for machinery, equivalent to 48.2 yuan in national currency. The price of diesel fuel this year is 80 yuan in national currency. After the implementation of the new tax, the price per ton will increase by 62.5 percent, almost two-thirds. Diesel fuel engines are used for agricultural irrigation, rice milling, oil extraction, river dredging, and as the original power source for small factories. They are not comparable to luxury goods. Once the tax is increased, the entire rural industrial sector will be greatly affected. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to the Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry, and submitted it to party headquarters at all levels, requesting the government to immediately stop the tax and allow the withdrawal of the order.

Yangzhou: Xu Dingkang Talks About Liutang River Project 104

Xu Dingkang, the director of the Canal Engineering Bureau, returned to the bureau by boat from Qing yesterday. He spoke in detail about the recent progress of the Liutang River project. He said that since the project started, it has been nearly two months. In these two months, he has convened several meetings with the county magistrates of the counties related to the river basin, discussed concrete plans, and submitted them to the province for approval and implementation. The construction in Dongtai, Guanyun, Lianshui, and Shuyang counties, where labor recruitment was difficult, has also begun in order. The general situation is on track. However, the weather is too cold, and the rivers are frozen, making the project difficult to carry out. The Qianji Dam in the upper reaches of the Liutang River has been completed, and the Longtou Dam in the lower reaches is scheduled to begin construction on the 10th of this month. The Chaimi Dam in the middle section is under construction. After the three dams are completed, dredging machines will be used to dredge the river channels in various places. It is reported that Director Xu will report the progress of the project to the province in the coming days.

Unable to Bear Family Burden, Husband and Wife Commit Suicide by Poison 105

Jin Zhengkai and his wife, residents of the Liao Family Village in Xiannvmiao, both in their fifties, had two sons. The eldest son, Jin Zhong, worked at the Hecheng Silk Shop on Duozi Street in Yangzhou. Because the Lunar New Year was approaching, the father went to Yangzhou to ask his son for money. The son, having no savings, negotiated with the shop owner and borrowed 20 yuan to take home. However, it was a drop in the bucket and not enough. The parents inevitably criticized him. Jin Zhong suddenly had suicidal thoughts. He went to the city, bought one yuan of opium, and returned home. Weeping, he told his wife, "I do not want to live in this world. Take care of yourself." Hearing this, the wife also wept and said, "I am willing to die with you." The husband and wife then swallowed the opium. At midnight, Jin Zhong's daughter suddenly cried out for her mother. The neighbor in the opposite room heard the crying and sensed something was wrong. He rushed in and saw the son and daughter-in-law lying in each other's arms. The son still had a breath. He quickly called the neighbors to give first aid with soap water. The son was saved. But the daughter-in-law had already died.

Siam Restricts Overseas Chinese 113

Increasing the Residence Fee to 100 Baht

A Central News Agency report states that in recent years, overseas Chinese compatriots have been subjected to abuse by local authorities in various places. The most notable example is the expulsion of Chinese in Mexico. Recently, Siam, in order to restrict the entry of overseas Chinese, has also increased the immigration residence fee. According to sources from the local overseas Chinese community, the Siamese government, to restrict immigration, promulgated immigration regulations in 1927, requiring all entrants, in addition to holding consular passports, to pay an entry continuation fee of 7.50 Tical (Siamese currency). Subsequently, in August 1931, it promulgated amended regulations, increasing the entry fee to 10 Baht, bringing the total to 15 Baht including the continuation fee. Later, it further increased the residence fee by 30 Baht, leading to a daily decrease in the number of overseas Chinese going to Siam. It is now learned that the government will further increase the immigration residence fee from 30 Baht to 100 Baht, scheduled for promulgation on March 1 and implementation on April 1. It also stipulates that entrants must be proficient in the Siamese language or their native language before being allowed to disembark. As for immigrants who leave Siam but still need to return, they must obtain a return permit before leaving the country, and the permit fee will also increase from 5 Baht to more than 20 Baht. Therefore, it is predicted that after the implementation of these measures, the number of overseas Chinese going to Siam will inevitably decrease sharply. The following is an investigation of the number of overseas Chinese entering Siam in the last five years: From 1928 to 1929, the number of entries was 880,433 and exits was 621,38. From 1929 to 1930, the number of entries was 705,52 and exits was 526,77. From 1930 to 1931, the number of entries was 763,69 and exits was 542,19. From 1931 to 1932, the number of entries was 695,49 and exits was 530,58. From 1932 to 1933, the number of entries was 138,16 and exits was 243,67.

Compatriots in the Northeast Are Still Enthusiastic About Promoting Domestic Goods 115

The Knitting Industry Association Relays a Letter from Northeast Carriers

Petitioning the Ministry of Industry to Order the Jianghai Customs to Exempt Export Taxes

Still Our Country's Territory, Please Do Not Treat it as a Foreign Land, The Shanghai Knitting Industry Association is petitioning the Ministry of Industry to review and exempt the export tax levied by the Customs on the four northeastern provinces. The original text is as follows: A petition is hereby submitted regarding the request. A letter from the member, China First Knitting Factory, states: We, the undersigned carriers from the Northeast, have been promoting your factory's products for many years. Since the rebellion in Liaoning, although the four northeastern provinces have fallen into the hands of rebels, our country has not relinquished sovereignty and it is still Chinese territory and should not be treated as a foreign land. However, there is something inexplicable: your factory has already been approved by the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance to pay the regular tax under the Machine-Made Western Goods Tax Regulations, without the need to pay export customs duties again, as is the case with Southeast Asian countries. Now, when goods are shipped to the four northeastern provinces, which our country has not relinquished, it is even worse than shipping to foreign ports in Southeast Asia, which is doubtful. Furthermore, when we ship your factory's products, in addition to paying the consolidated tax and export tax, we also have to pay a landing tax upon arrival in the Northeast. In total, the various taxes are equivalent to the price of the goods. The cost is too high, making it difficult to sell. We have the intention to promote domestic goods, but lack the means to maintain it. We ask you to find a way to remedy this, otherwise we can only lament helplessly. We dare to state this directly, hoping for good news soon. Based on this, your factory has been approved by the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance for special treatment in accordance with the current measures of the Machine-Made Western Goods Tax, adhering to the principle of not levying taxes twice on the same item, to show preferential treatment. All domestic goods factories are the same. The collection of landing taxes in the Northeast is due to the rebel party controlling the government, and it is impossible to correct it. However, the collection of export taxes in Shanghai seems to be an exception. It is a misunderstanding of the meaning of promoting domestic goods and violates the principle of not levying taxes twice on the same item. We hope that your association, leading the industry, has always aimed to reduce the cost of products. The Northeast is still our country's territory, please do not treat it as a foreign land. We should separately review and transfer this to exempt the Shanghai export tax, so that the future of domestic goods will be greatly benefited. Based on this, in addition to replying in a letter, we should report the situation to the Ministry of Industry and request that it review and approve it, in accordance with the special treatment of the current measures of the Machine-Made Western Goods Tax, adhering to the principle of not levying taxes twice on the same item. It should be clearly ordered to the Jianghai Customs to exempt export taxes on goods destined for the Northeast, which would be a convenient law.

According to a report from the Central News Agency, there are rumors that the national treasury is depleted and that Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi will borrow funds from the Shanghai banking sector. After this loan is completed, the Ministry of Finance will not borrow funds from the banking sector again before June of this year. As for the 10 million yuan of customs treasury bonds of the 23rd year of the Republic, they have been deposited in the Central Bank treasury to offset previous debts.

(Note) When requesting, the number of the water bill and the location of the property must be stated. (2) Based on the reduction plan formulated by the company, repair any damaged water pipes immediately. If tenants in the property have a large amount of non-household water consumption (such as factories, restaurants, old-fashioned stoves, and other small businesses), please ask the company to install auxiliary water meters at the tenant's location. (Note) Special attention should be paid to the fact that the water company will select several locations for free installation of these auxiliary water meters. (3) Please ask the water company to provide printed notices to warn tenants not to waste and abuse the supplied water. (Note) These notices should be applied to the house. (4) Property owners should consider whether it is appropriate to install separate water meters for each tenant. After the installation of separate water meters for each tenant, the water company will directly enter into contracts with each user and collect water fees. (Note) If you want to install separate water meters for each tenant, the cost of all necessary changes to the water pipes should be borne by the property owner, and the property owner should also pay a cash deposit sufficient to cover the value of the water meter. The amount of this deposit has recently been reduced. A half-inch (1/2") water meter now costs only 47 yuan, and a three-eighths inch (3/8") water meter costs 33 yuan. If you want to know the total amount of the deposit required for each property, you can inquire with the water company, which will be happy to inform you. For trial purposes, the company has tried a new method of meter installation, which can greatly reduce the cost of changing water pipes. Although there may be a loss of interest on the water meter deposit, it is very small compared to the water bill savings after installing meters in places with excessive water bills. Please note that this deposit will be refunded when the property is transferred or the water meter is removed. (In addition, there are several drawings and descriptions (auxiliary water meters) of the differences between (separate household water meters) and new meter installation methods, (omitted).
