Grain Market: Foreign Wheat Prices Rise, Standard Flour Market Soars 208

Yesterday in the flour market, after the opening of the morning session, market conditions for all months were consistently strong. Foreign wheat quotes: Chicago rose by about 34 cents, Canada rose by 45 cents. Therefore, after the opening price, market sentiment in all months was unusually firm. January to March became gradually more active with more speculators. Speculators deliberately pushed up prices, significantly better than the previous week. By the fourth session in the afternoon, market sentiment remained high. This month's price reached a high of two yuan and two cents, while March and April also reached a high of two yuan, one cent and nine and a half cents. Then, factories suddenly came out to sell off, causing market sentiment to fall back by one or two cents. However, long-term contracts remained steady due to very thin trading. As a result, this month remained unchanged, March fell by 7.5%, April fell by 1%, May fell by 5%, June rose by 5%, and July rose by 1.5%. Spot wheat: Fuxin sold 776 bags of Yaowan wheat for 4.1 yuan, and Jiangxi wheat for 3.86 yuan. In addition, Fufeng sold two ships of US wheat from the government, and Huafeng sold 1,000 tons, both at a price of 4.25 yuan.

Southern and Northern Rice Industries Agree to End Temporary Halt on the 9th 209

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, over fifty sources from various groups (over 7,000 stones) showed signs of weakness at the opening. Local shops took little interest, and there was no improvement until near noon. Regular groups such as Su Tong's japonica continued to fall by 5 cents, and Du Yangjian also fell by nearly 10 cents. Various groups of late rice, from Northern Ocean, Tianjin, Tanggu and other groups,

progressively traded over three thousand bags, and the market slightly turned around, but the price only increased by two cents. Yin Bianyuan had no wide outlets, and its shape and color were fatigued, causing the price to fall by around 10 cents. Furthermore, according to a joint resolution by the Shanghai Northern and Southern Rice Groups, the market will close on the 9th of this month to facilitate a major settlement, and a group worship ceremony will be held on the 18th. The reopening date will be discussed and announced at the meeting on the 18th. (North Shanghai) Thirty-two or three shipments from various routes arrived, but the market remained stagnant. Bagged rice was discounted to stimulate movement. Few transactions were made by each household. High-quality white japonica was flat and weak, and medium-grade rice was discounted by around 10 cents. Du Jian, Bo Dao, Early Rice, and Ke Jian were stable.

Ke Xian Rice Vendors Have Already Stopped Selling 210

｜Only 150 Bags Opened in the Unified Market｜

Yesterday, Ke Xian rice was approaching the end of the Lunar New Year, and all parties were seeking to close positions. Both arrivals and sales were low, and inventories were slightly higher. Vendors wanted to hold until the red market next spring and were currently unwilling to sell. While outlets in Fuzhou had stopped, Quanzhou was still interested, but due to depleted floating stocks, trading was not smooth. In the unified market, only 150 bags of Jiangbei machine-milled Xian rice were sold to Quanzhou, with the price at 7 yuan, one yuan higher than the previous market. There were no other transactions. However, there were still ample stocks of foreign rice in the market. Yesterday, a Zhejiang group inquired, and it is likely that there will be some direct allocations during the Lunar New Year.

Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cakes Gradually Ending 211

Miscellaneous grains and oil cake businesses are mostly closing down due to the approaching end of the lunar year. Therefore, the market in the Miscellaneous Grains Association and the Caishutang was quiet, with sparse transactions. Total transactions included over a hundred bags of peanuts, over seven hundred bags of wheat, and five carts of eight hundred bags of soybeans. Among these, there were also goods bought by dealers. Oil included six hundred pieces of Jiacang raw oil and fifty pieces of Lunlianqi soybean oil. Currently, there are no changes expected in the market conditions for various commodities.

White Tung Oil Exports Not Strong Last Month 212

The white tung oil market is primarily centered in Hubei, and the export volume last month seemed lower than the previous month. The approximate total was just over a thousand tons. Market price fluctuations were limited. The highest price for January was only 25 yuan, and the lowest was 22.7 yuan, a difference of only 2.3 yuan. The average was around 23.6 yuan. Because foreign firms did not handle large quantities, fluctuations were small. At the end of the month, American foreign firms made some purchases, and the selling price was 23.2 yuan. Then, Hubei firms wanted to increase the price, apparently requiring 23.6 or 7 yuan before they would sell. The foreign firms were unwilling to do so, so the deal did not close. By the beginning of this month, the price was still only 23.2 yuan, and there were some transactions. Therefore, the rumors in Shanghai that Hubei was reporting good conditions were only empty talk and there were no real transactions taking place. The current market is like this, and because the settlement period is approaching, there is likely to be no change in market conditions. It is heard that Hubei dealers bought Hubei tung oil for slightly more than 19 yuan, and Wenchou, including taxes, was only 18.6 or 7 yuan. The after-market may increase slightly, but it is not known. This is probably due to the small number of sellers. Local firms are in the process of closing, and there have been very few transactions recently. Zhejiang tung oil is gradually becoming cheaper. A few days ago, the Hangzhou market traded at 19.1 or 2 yuan for Jiangsu delivery.

Metals: Metal Merchants Rush to Close Accounts 213

With the end of the lunar year approaching, metal merchants are rushing to close their accounts. As a result, there is very little buying and selling in the market. Market prices have not changed significantly. However, some factories are still absorbing futures contracts for the next regular period. It is heard that tinplate, cement, rebar, and factory-made nails are all being bought, but the quantities are not as large as usual.

Silk and Tea: Actively Selling Raw Silk 214

(Report of Rising Prices for Jia Ang Bai Factory Silk): The Lyon raw silk market has recently seen a surge in silk prices due to the start of spring sales. Chinese silk, such as Grade B white factory silk, is already open at 68.75 francs, up 1.25 francs per kilogram. Sichuan and Shandong yellow factory silk have also risen by half a franc.

(Yellow and White Factory Silk Continuously Transported to Hangzhou): The yellow and white factory silk purchased by silk merchants in Shanghai last month is now being transported to Hangzhou. In the last three days, 125 bales have been transported from Shanghai to Hangzhou by train.

(European Sales of Factory Silk Gradually Becoming Active): Overseas sales of Chinese factory silk are gradually increasing. Telegrams from Lyon and other places are gradually being forwarded to Shanghai. European firms are taking the opportunity to purchase yellow and white factory silk, and transactions are not limited. Xinfu and others have purchased a total of 75 bales of Grade A spot goods, and prices have been rising steadily.

Piece Goods and Woolens in the Process of Closing 215

As the end of the year approaches, the trade in woolen fabrics is becoming increasingly sluggish. Inventories are being checked and accounts are being settled in order to close the books and prepare for a new year. Recently, the market for various thick and thin woolen fabrics has been virtually stagnant. Even the business of clothing shops that sell piece goods is now much worse, showing signs of closing down. Ordinary winter woolens have already been purchased by customers. However, ready-made coats for men and women still have considerable business recently. The prices are on average one cent cheaper than ten days ago.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

A Serious Problem 235

— Ya Fei

This is by no means an ordinary piece of news, but a serious problem concerning the future of Shanghai! Yesterday, I opened a certain evening newspaper and saw a shocking headline in a special font, which stated: "The city market is declining and business is sluggish. Recently, more than 500 large and small shops have been sued for debt and have applied to the court for enforcement of closure; many are on Nanjing Road. The current authorities are considering this, because a rash execution would have a huge impact on the entire Shanghai market..." The day before yesterday, I visited Wang Qun, a business tycoon in this city, on business, and we talked about the current commercial situation in Shanghai. He said: "Since the January 28th Incident, the city market has become increasingly depressed. The increase in rents has made it difficult for ordinary merchants to bear. In addition, the rural economy is bankrupt, and various countries are also experiencing depression, financial difficulties, and reduced purchasing power. In these turbulent times, maintaining the status quo is already a very difficult task, let alone development! Although, from the surface, Shanghai seems to be thriving recently, with magnificent ten-story buildings, grand cinemas, large hotels, dance halls, and banks springing up like mushrooms after a rain. But if you observe from the side, I believe that these are all abnormal developments and should not be considered good phenomena. They symbolize the crisis of Shanghai's future. According to my accurate estimation, the number of businesses in this city that will close down by the end of the lunar year will not be small..." I think, if the above two pieces of news are true, then isn't Shanghai really going to collapse? But, in my opinion, these are not unfounded words, and it is indeed a serious problem! However, the obstacles that create this problem are nothing more than the following six reasons.

(The gift of the January 28th Incident) Since the January 28th Incident, when the Japanese army committed atrocities in Zhabei, more than half of Shanghai's market was destroyed by artillery fire. Although the concessions barely maintained a normal state (?), the market has since been in a slump, and financial turnover has been sluggish. Those big capitalists are also in a state of desperation, and most of the small capitalists are unable to maintain themselves and have fallen into decline one after another. Only a few are able to barely survive. (The global economic depression) The wave of the global economic depression has hit China, and the business community has been the first to bear the brunt, directly and indirectly suffering its great impact. Because our country has been plagued by foreign aggression and internal strife for several years, and has also suffered from natural and man-made disasters, the squeeze of great power aggression, and the exploitation of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies. It was already full of holes and had lost its vitality, how could it withstand the pressure of this depression!

(The bankruptcy of the rural economy) Our country has always been recognized by countries around the world as an agricultural country, so the countryside has become the lifeline of our country, especially the source of life for the business community. Once the countryside goes bankrupt, the national commercial market will also collapse. This is undoubtedly true. In recent years, our country's rural areas have been plagued by floods, droughts, wars, and banditry, one after another, and agricultural products have also suffered from a sharp decline. The silk and tea, which farmers regard as a major source of income, have also plummeted. There are no rich households in the villages, and there are starving people on the roads. The distant causes and near consequences are not a matter of a day or two. How great is its relationship with commerce!

(The decline in purchasing power) Because of the bankruptcy of the countryside, the economic turnover is sluggish. Purchasing power is also decreasing day by day, which has dealt a huge blow to the business operations of various business communities. Merchants originally rely entirely on people's purchases to maintain their lives, but now the decline in purchasing power is tantamount to monopolizing the source of their lives.

(Senseless competition) Because of the sluggish business, they compete with each other by lowering prices, hoping to attract customers and increase their purchasing power. Therefore, in the streets and alleys, in front of stores large and small, the banners of big discounts and big giveaways are often hung up all year round. The decorative consumption of one kind is bound to be an alarming number when calculated. But this method is only like a dying person taking a shot of adrenaline, just to prolong this moment of life. Fundamentally, isn't it still the same hopeless?

(The unbearable burden of rent) At present, the price of real estate in Shanghai is only being raised as much as possible, and those big landlords, in order to protect their own interests, have no choice but to produce on the tenants! So they desperately increase the rent, regardless of the strength of the tenants, whether they can afford these or not, they just squeeze them heavily. The income of ordinary merchants in one month of business is not enough to pay for one month of rent. Therefore, they inevitably go into debt and go bankrupt. Those who made money in previous years can still struggle a little. If it is a newly opened business or one without a foundation, it is impossible to gain a foothold!

From the above six reasons, I infer that the more than five hundred stores being sued are indeed in a situation of helplessness, and they really have unspeakable pain. If the authorities rashly execute them according to the requirements of the plaintiffs, the impact on the entire city of Shanghai will be unimaginable. If the authorities, in order to take care of the city's market, do not execute them, then in the future, once this trend starts, it will also cause great resentment! I don't know how the authorities will deal with this difficult case in a satisfactory way.

The voices of the rent reduction movement in the past few days have spread throughout the city. This is good news to hear; I wonder what the outcome will be in the future? Let us wait quietly for the arrival of this good news!

Beside the Garbage Dump 236

— Li Zhai

One pile, two piles... Mountains of gray garbage piled up, filling this desolate square, scattered and disorderly. From a distance, it looked just like a cemetery in an ossuary where graves were mass-buried.

The clear morning sun gradually shone into the square. Wisps of heat rose from the garbage piles, emitting a strange, sour, and moldy odor.

(Wooo)! After a while, a yellow garbage truck occasionally came speeding, and clouds of dust and mist filled the sky, like dark clouds. The children all raised an arm to cover their eyes.

There are especially many children here, and they are all dressed in such tattered and dirty clothes. Although it is the cold winter, some are still barefoot. They are innocent and lively, jumping around. From their oily black faces and ragged clothes, it is clear that they are the children of the poor. They all have parents and families, but because of poverty, they are not qualified to enjoy "modern education" like the little "darlings" and "brothers". Every day, from early morning until dusk, they are just immersed in this only "park"—the desolate square—burying their golden childhood in the garbage dump.

The strange odor emitted from the huge garbage piles attracts them. This is the only old theater stage, the natural battlefield, and the fascinating gambling factory. Here, there are often the footprints of great men such as "Emperor", "King", "Wu Song", and "Zhang Fei". Large-scale, organized fierce battles often erupt. They play marbles and cards, and even forget to go home for dinner because of small gambles for a few pennies. Here, there is also cunning, treachery, deception, and power. This is a miniature world, a free gathering place for poor children.

Three or four children are surrounding a pile of new garbage in the left corner. Each is holding a bamboo stick or a short rod, dragging and scratching. Carefully and attentively, they are looking for discarded waste that is still slightly valuable—scrap iron, rags, empty cans, etc.—to supplement the meager income of their poor families.

(Oh)! Little Gouzi, who was ten years old, suddenly jumped up while dragging and scratching in a trance. (What?)? Little Qizi and Zhaodi next to him were both stunned by this unusual shout. They asked in unison. (Money) Little Gouzi said, revealing the pattern of a banknote from the gap between the fingers of a tightly clenched hand. (Let me see)! Little Qizi stretched out his left hand a long way. (No way! I picked it up) Little Gouzi shook his head and took two steps back. (You won't even let me see it)? Little Qizi said, glancing at Zhaodi next to him, taking two steps forward, his chest puffed up, his right hand tightly grasping the broken stool leg used to drag the garbage, just like an officer of an imperial power holding a command knife. The situation was about to turn violent.

(It doesn't matter if you take a look! Anyway, no one wants your money). Zhaodi was, after all, a girl, and her tone was more slick.

Little Gouzi hesitated! He thought that if it was just Zhaodi, he wouldn't be afraid. To deal with a girl, he only needed to grab her yellow and short braid, and all problems would be solved. But Little Qizi was a tough one. Not to mention that he was a head taller than him, that thick and hard stool leg would be at least a little uncomfortable if it hit his waist. Moreover, Little Qizi had just winked at Zhaodi, definitely negotiating some secret diplomacy, preparing to rob him of his banknote and split it in half. Under this serious situation, rather than resisting at the cost of losing the banknote and suffering physical pain, it would be better to respectfully offer it with both hands. If Little Qizi and Zhaodi occasionally discovered a little "humanity" or "conscience", there might still be a few percent hope of consolation.

(It's okay to look, but no one is allowed to rob). Little Gouzi was, after all, smart. In the end, he decided to adopt a policy of non-resistance, but his tone absolutely concealed his weakness.

Little Gouzi loosened his hand holding the banknote, and six eyes stared at the banknote like hungry wolves.

(A fake banknote, for the devils)! Little Qizi and Zhaodi discovered that it was a five-dollar

fake banknote. Not only was the pattern very blurred, but a corner of the banknote was also burned black. (Ha! Hurry up and take it back for your mom to use) Zhaodi sarcastically mocked.

Everything was destroyed! Little Qizi's contemptuous smile and Zhaodi's mocking sarcasm made Little Gouzi feel extremely humiliated. This humiliation was more vicious than cursing his mother or his ancestors for thirteen generations. It was a permanent and indelible disgrace.

Little Gouzi's tears flowed unconsciously to his cheeks. He didn't know whether he was sad or indignant! He fiercely tore the banknote in half and threw it on the ground, lowered his head, and quietly left the square with a weeping face. Finally, he only heard him say softly, (No one said it was real)!

Human Cleverness 237

— Bin Fu

(Humans are the most intelligent of all beings). Yes, humans are indeed the most intelligent animals in the universe. However, even among these (intelligent animals), there is a natural division between the wise and the foolish. At least, I think I am one of the most foolish among this group of (intelligent animals).

Once, I had to go from the western district to the eastern district for some business, so I took a tram. The tram was extremely crowded. Not only were all the seats taken, but even those standing in the middle of the aisle were jostling back and forth, everyone with red faces, struggling desperately. I stood beside the tram door, one hand pinching a coin, the other resting on the door to support myself. As the tram approached a certain stop, a fashionable young man struggled out of the crowd, his face so solemn, as if he was very resentful of my hand resting on the door. He forcefully flung my hand away, sliding the door open with a bang. My hand landed in the door seam, holding it open. After he got out, he immediately slammed the door shut. This time, my fingers were caught. I was in so much pain that I wanted to cry, instinctively pulling my hand back and examining the flowing blood. At this moment, the young man was still standing on the platform, glaring at me ferociously through the glass, muttering:

(Damn it! Doesn't know what's good for him!)

I wrapped my injured finger with a handkerchief, enduring double the pain. After a while, the conductor finally took the coins I had already counted, threw them into the coin bag, and said: (Sorry, wait a moment), then went to the back.

When the tram arrived at another stop, another young man stood up from a seat next to a burly man. In his haste, he stepped on the burly man's outstretched foot. The burly man's eyes widened, and he said loudly: (Are you blind? Damn it!)

The young man kept saying (I'm sorry) while bending down to dust off the man's foot. The burly man then grunted (forget it), and the young man got off the tram in a fluster.

The tram was about to reach my destination, but the ticket had not yet arrived. I was worried about (the conductor), worried that (the ticket inspector) would be coming soon. I wanted to ask him for the ticket several times, but I finally hesitated and didn't say anything. Later, I couldn't bear the worry any longer, so I took the opportunity to tug at (the conductor) and gently asked:

(Can I have the ticket now? Hey.) (It's alright, I know!) (The conductor) smiled and looked out the window, then walked to the back again.

(The ticket inspector) finally came. I was really worried about (the conductor) because I felt it was his responsibility.

The ticket inspector asked me for my ticket, so I pointed anxiously at the conductor. (The ticket inspector) shouted: (Number XXX, where's the ticket!) (What? Did he ever buy a ticket?) (The conductor), with his hat pushed back and his mouth full of saliva, said fiercely.

(Well, I did buy it.) I don't know why, but my face felt a little hot, and I couldn't speak loudly.

(How much? Buy it now! I saw you just get on!) (The conductor) said aggressively. (A few coins don't matter, but I really did buy it. I might as well buy another one now.) I took out the coins and gave them to the ticket inspector, asking him to give me change. I thought (the conductor) should understand.

(Hmph! Who wants your handout?) The conductor continued to grumble. At this moment, I got off the tram in silence, still hearing (the ticket inspector) and the driver scolding:

(What a grievance! If you can't afford the tram, don't take it!)

I stood on the street, stroking my aching finger, and I was lost. Afterwards, I thought of vowing never to take the tram again. But my friend T said to me: (Bin, you're too stupid! Do you still want to live in this world? Open your eyes and look at the whole world. Isn't everything like this? To avoid it, you only have to not live!)

Then I realized, now I know "This is the cleverness humans should have." I also want to learn to be smarter in the future, because I still want to live.

Sending a Couplet to Celebrate the Old Year 238

— Fei Shi

I remember (Modern) once published a couplet written by Mr. Yu Dafu himself, which read: (Avoiding my seat, I fear hearing of literary inquisitions. Writing books is all for rice and sustenance.) It roughly quoted a line from Gong Ding'an's poetry. Mr. Yu Dafu is a famous writer.

Judging by his background, he can also be considered to come from a distinguished family. Naturally, his own position here is not inferior to the masses, and moreover, Mr. Dafu has been a true literati from beginning to end, without any ambition to (usurp power) or rebellious intentions to (rise up in revolt). Logically, he should have been able to enjoy his quiet life. However, he had such feelings. As for the general public who stand below Mr. Dafu, the extent of their feelings is needless to say. From this, we can gauge the climate of our country.

Now it is time for the Lunar New Year again. Although the government has long issued an order to abolish it, even in Shanghai, this center of civilization, the general public still paste red couplets on their doors and set off firecrackers during this period to express welcoming the new and sending off the old. Firecrackers are uniform, the most uniform thing being the sound of firecrackers. Red couplets, however, vary in style, especially the ones pasted on the doors of so-called scholarly families, which undergo the greatest changes. Moreover, many of them change with the changes in national affairs and political situations at that time. But I wonder if there are still such scholarly families? If there are, then please paste this couplet recorded by Mr. Dafu.

Literati are generally only able to grumble, so as the saying goes: (A scholar's rebellion will not succeed in three years.) However, literati who can grumble are ultimately more promising. In the past, many literati, because they suffered from not having a place to use their talents, inevitably vented some of their grievances in couplets. However, now even this is not easy to see.

When I was a child, I only felt that red paper with black characters pasted on the door was much better looking than the original black door frame, and I was also very happy because it told me that I would be wearing new clothes and eating good food. After entering school, I learned that there were many meanings to them. However, in general, there was no significant change. It wasn't! (Heaven increases years, man increases lifespan, spring fills the universe, fortune fills the door), or! (Spring flowers, spring wine, spring wealth, fortune, prosperity, longevity, auspiciousness), almost every year it was these words.

This year, as the second anniversary of the January 28th Incident passes, with many bloodstains still blurred in our hearts, the Lunar New Year arrives. I might as well send everyone a couplet to congratulate them on this (prosperous year) that should be filled with joy: (National affairs are unbearable to discuss, so let's not discuss national affairs. Family matters are mostly sighing, so let's just sigh about family matters.)

An Introduction to the Philosophy of Borrowing Money 239

— Mai Fu

Usually, when you go to someone to borrow money, you always say half of what you want to say, leaving the other half for the other person to figure out. Saying half and leaving half for people to think about naturally requires the use of so-called presentation techniques. Because even a single bone fragment can reveal the whole body of a beast, but that requires specialized knowledge. However, few people prepare such specialized knowledge for the convenience of others borrowing money, so this is where misunderstandings arise in the world.

Originally, not using techniques is certainly not good, but if techniques are used excessively, people can become confused. Because saying half doesn't lead to loss of status, making people look down on you. However, for the sake of taking out your own money and cutting out your own flesh, even if you pretend to be foolish or ignorant to get by, that's probably what you hope for. Because everyone has their own reasons, and these reasons occur frequently, so those who borrow money, regardless of whether they leave too much for people to think about, or just the right amount, if there is no result, they will always think that people are deliberately confusing them.

And the other party, regardless of whether they hear the unsaid implications, or they really don't understand what's going on, they generally dismiss it lightly, rejoicing that they have avoided being robbed. This will always easily lead to resentment, and once resentment arises, they will always want to retaliate against the other party. So, among the so-called kidnappers, I'm afraid there are quite a few such gentlemen who borrow money.

The Lonely Man (7) 241

— Dai Ni

(4) Wedding March. Spring, the days pass by like flying. But as Kejia and Jingyi hate the long nights, the spring breeze still quickly sends away three days. On this third morning, readers should come to attend this wedding. In front of a large hotel next to the racecourse, five-colored ribbons flutter in the March spring breeze. Waiters in white uniforms shuttle back and forth like shuttles. We walk forward from the aisle and can see Xiaosun wearing a nervous smile, shaking hands and nodding to every guest. Among the female guests, Jingwen is naturally indispensable.

The wedding ceremony is the newest style. In the center of the living room is a long table covered with white cloth and a marriage certificate. When the bride and groom arrive by car, the ceremony will be held here to perform the (play) that adorns life.

A pair of mismatched guests walked in from the outside. Although the man was dressed up so nicely, his age made people feel that there was an irreconcilable regret in this couple. I will now introduce to the readers that the woman is Qinbo, and the man is, needless to say, her husband. When she came in, she seemed to pay special attention to Xiaosun. He jumped over, patted her shoulder and said, (Xiaosun, it's rare that you came back from Hangzhou.) Xiaosun was facing inside, talking to a friend. Startled, he turned around, saw that it was Qinbo, and seemed stunned as if he hadn't expected her to come. But he busied himself naturally and shook her hand. (Long time no see, Qinbo, it's rare that you came so early.) Nervously smiling. (Haven't met, have you?) She saw her husband standing beside her. (Mr. Zhu Xiaosun! Li Shaoqin) They shook hands, and nods represented greetings. Jingwen heard Qinbo's voice and ran over to greet her. (I thank you on behalf of my sister.) (Naughty child, I asked Jingyi a few days ago and she said you hadn't come to Shanghai yet.) (I couldn't get a substitute teacher, I really don't want to do this kind of thing.) Xiaosun stood beside her, shaking his naturally curly hair. Jingwen seemed to suddenly remember something and said: (My mother wants to meet you!) She let go of Qinbo's hand. (I won't entertain you.) Xiaosun and Li Shaoqin nodded, and the two of them went hand in hand to the temporary bridal chamber. Jingwen's mother was a kind middle-aged woman. Seeing the two of them smiling and entering, she stood up and asked: (Is this Mr. Zhu?) (Yes, younger brother...my mother.) (Auntie.) (Mr. Zhu, please don't laugh, I'm still like a child at such an old age.) One smiled innocently, and the other shook his naturally curly hair. (Thank you very much, Mr. Zhu, for coming all the way from Hangzhou to help.)

(It's right to come and congratulate you. Auntie.) (I heard that Mr. Zhu is recuperating in Hangzhou, is your health better now?) (Thank you, Auntie, it's better now.)

(Then after Kejia's wedding, you won't go back to Hangzhou?) Jingwen's mother lengthened her tone as if she had some hope, while looking at her daughter. (That's not certain...probably not going.) (Kejia said that there are too many empty rooms in his new house and he doesn't want to post rental notices. I've already agreed to move in with Jingwen. If Mr. Zhu can live in Shanghai, then we'll have even more fun.)

(That's naturally very good, almost all our own people! Um, better to be with close friends.) (It'll be even more fun when Mr. Zhu gets married.) The old lady said jokingly. Xiaosun nervously lowered his head and shook his naturally curly hair. The sound of military music rang out outside. The old lady said to Jingwen: (They're here!)

Movie Supplement

Katherine Hepburn's Novelty and Uniqueness 242

=Good at lies, even she says it's unreliable= =Eccentric behavior, a belly full of bad ideas= This Katherine Hepburn, who is called an American guest, is unfortunately called a substitute for Garbo because her face is somewhat like that of the Swedish star. In fact, she has her own special personality and her own artistic strengths, and she did not become famous by looking like a foreign star. Now, most actresses are following the trend of fashion, without the courage to develop their personal characteristics. Therefore, I have specially brought up the various unique points of this Katherine Hepburn, which may be of considerable benefit to the general actresses in China. Of course, Katherine also has various quirks that are not worth learning from, but isn't that an unavoidable metamorphosis in the midst of an actress's transformation? This Katherine Hepburn can also be called a strange star. She has been in Hollywood for so long, and her past life and family background have not yet been exposed. What she tells people today, she denies tomorrow. The most interesting thing is that she herself said that she has given birth to two children; her husband is called Ludlow Smith. But now she seems to deny it again. One day, she said to a reporter, (Okay, you can announce this news. Yes, I have children, I have two. It's really interesting. Of course, they all have pitch-black faces...you should also announce this for me.) You think this kind of talk is humorous enough, but if you meet a straightforward person who believes it, wouldn't it cause a big joke? Before Katherine came to Hollywood, she had already carefully examined everything in Hollywood. She knew that what Hollywood needed most at that time was strangeness and novelty. So she brought a big bag of strangeness and novelty to Hollywood. When she first arrived, the outside world had already released enough rumors, saying that she was a rich young lady, and that she had millions of her own property, etc. In this way, her reputation spread throughout the United States. She also has various eccentric behaviors in Hollywood, such as liking to wear worker's overalls, and she specially asked famous tailors to add a few patches to them. She often reads letters sent to her by fans in the middle of the road. She also likes to talk to a monkey she keeps. She often wears only a very small pair of shorts besides her top. She is so strangely shaped, but she doesn't think it's strange at all.

People say she is very innocent, but she is too innocent. She often has a nose full of freckles, but after a few days, the freckles are no longer visible. It turns out that her freckles are not very obvious, but sometimes she deliberately deepens them with an eyebrow pencil, which makes the freckles more obvious. Isn't this too much innocence? One day, she suddenly had a strange idea and wanted to play golf. No one had ever seen her golf skills, but she played very well as soon as she hit the ball. She even dared to challenge Eileen Dunn, a female golf expert. This is also very strange. In short, she is like a magician who performs magic tricks, but no one can guess whether she has rabbits or chickens hidden in her hat. Even she herself admits that she is an unreliable liar. But she can play any role like anyone else, she does everything well, and she can do everything well. Aren't these all the skills that an all-around actress must have?

Audience Opinions

Feelings on (Life) 243

— Lv Yi

(Life) is a work with a novel style, containing profound stimulation and educational significance. Ruan Lingyu and Lin Chuchu are models of two types of women, and at the same time, they can be said to be models of two mothers. Ruan Lingyu's life (in the furnace of life, a fragile soul is tempered, tempered, and tempered) has suffered setbacks and tribulations. She sincerely understands the unwillingness of an inhuman life, but she cannot find a bright path in the dark journey of life, and finally ends her life in a muddle. In the current society, there are many women who have groped in the dark for a lifetime like this, and (Life) reminds them. Lin Chuchu, on the other hand, is a human mother who regards educating children as a lifelong task. She abandons all desires and devotes her life's energy to educating children. But this kind of ideal woman is probably forever in the realm of ideals!

The author also raised the issue of social education and family education. He explained that for a person's thoughts, behaviors, and character, social education and family education are more important than school education. The advantages and disadvantages of the social and family environment have an infinitely great influence on people. Everyone knows this, but everyone has been confused about it. This is worthy of serious attention by educators in general.

Speaking again of the issue of a young man's way out. It is extremely proper for a young man to be dissatisfied with his own life and seek a long-term way out. But what should be carefully noted is to be careful not to step into dangerous territory, or even find a dead end. The young man in (Life) is an example. He sought a way out because he was not used to the hard life of an elementary school teacher, but as a result, he ended up committing suicide. This is an excellent lesson for young people. In short, after watching (Life), it is as if you have heard a philosophical lesson. Recalling it, there is infinite pleasure.

What Does (Life) Taste Like? 244

— Yu Bi

A (woman) went from being a (wild child), (maid), (female worker) to becoming a (prostitute), and she still thought she had tasted all the flavors of (life). An elementary school teacher, he felt that his (life) was too ordinary, so he left his wife to find a new path in the big city. Unexpectedly, he and she were combined, and a year later, they had a child. She thought that she had lived a hard life for half her life and should enjoy it, so she gradually could not maintain it, which led him astray. He thought of the life of the child, so he wrote a letter to his ex-wife, asking her to take care of the child, and he threw himself into the sea to end their (life). She, who had drifted all her life, finally realized and took a child without a mother as her son. She thought of her own son, so she went to hug him and live with this child. Because of different education, the children quarreled. So her own son was taken away by her husband's ex-wife again. Fifteen years have passed, she is old and was driven out by a man with a son. Where is her home? She did not have the courage to see her own son, and finally, one day, she fell to the ground and died, ending her (life). What does (life) taste like? The taste of (life) is originally a packet of bitter water.

Review of (Passionate Youth) 245

— Ke Luo

This film takes promoting national goods and resisting foreign goods as the center of its ideology, which seems to be very correct; however, it actually distorts the facts and obscures the truth, making people think of (malicious propaganda) immediately after watching it.

The story describes how great the authority of the goods (note: it does not specify (enemy) goods or (Japanese) goods here) inspection association is, and how enthusiastic the public security bureau is in cracking down on counterfeit goods. If this is really the case, then what else can we say? It's just that what we actually see is the foreign goods inspection association being dissolved and disbanded, the inspectors being arrested and imprisoned, and the unimpeded sales of enemy goods in our country. These are ironclad facts!

Therefore, we see it how it is far away from reality and dreaming vaguely. That mediocre and despicable preaching makes people want to vomit!

As for the technical aspects, they are still not satisfactory. Although the director used many small clever tricks—such as using the child to discover the hole in his father's shoe to show his poverty, and using long cigarette ash to show

Li Accountant's anxiety: these are all very good—however, in the end, they are just small clever tricks. There are many scenes in the photography that are unacceptable, such as when Kejian went to investigate counterfeit goods at night, the light was no different from daytime! The actors all seemed a bit stiff. Zhang Zhenduo, who played Diao Renzhi, was very flexible and competent, but in many places he was very pretentious. Kejian's sick mother had no signs of illness, and was obviously pretending to be sick there. Ye Qiuxin is just an ordinary character in this film and has not been fully expressed.

Cang Yinqiu Misses Her Relatives on the Holiday 246

— Background Board

(Alone as a stranger in a foreign land, I miss my relatives all the more on every holiday. I know my brothers are climbing to the high places, wearing dogwood, missing one person.) This is a poem about missing relatives on holidays in Tang poetry. The lines write out the heart of a traveler, which can be said to be extremely thorough. Unexpectedly, the old man's poem has become a portrayal of modern people. There is an actress in the film industry, Cang Yinqiu. A few years ago, she came to Shanghai from Henan alone. Although she relied on her intelligence and hard work, she has now occupied a place in the film industry, but she is alone and wandering in a foreign land. The white clouds and the setting moon often make her think of her hometown. Sometimes, she even forgets to eat and sleep, which is really a regrettable thing.

A few days ago, I met Miss Cang Yinqiu at Yihua Company. From her mouth, I learned that she has a role in (Woman), and it is a role that suits her personality. When we were talking, suddenly a burst of explosive sound came from outside. Cang Yinqiu heard it and asked: (Is this the sound of firecrackers?)

A person next to her immediately replied: (Not bad, it's just those stubborn villagers who are celebrating the harvest.) Who knew that this sentence was not serious, but it touched the heart of this thoughtful girl Cang Yinqiu. She immediately showed a solemn expression on her face, motionless, and seemed to be thinking about something. Everyone looked at her and felt very strange, so they asked each other why she was suddenly standing there in a daze? Cang Yinqiu then said indifferently: (I'm alone in Shanghai. Every time I spend the New Year, I always shed tears several times! It turns out that you don't know that my parents are still waiting for me in my hometown...), she said here, and her eyes seemed to be a little wet! The many people who heard this all lowered their heads, and the air immediately became quiet. Naturally, everyone expressed their deep sympathy for Cang Yinqiu.

Film Novel

Christina the Queen (5) 247

— Watson

The young imperial envoy asked Christina again: "How much further is it to the nearest inn?" Christina laughed and said, "It's still more than six miles. By the time you get there, it will be night. Of course, you wouldn't want to get stuck in a ditch again." The young man bowed deeply and said, "Thank you for your kindness." He assumed Christina was a boy because she was wearing men's clothing, so he instructed his servant, "Peter, give this child a gold pound." After saying that, he went back into the carriage. Christina took a gold pound from the servant's hand. She smiled and turned the gold pound over and over in her hand, looking at it. On the gold pound was engraved her own face, and around it were the words "Her Majesty Queen Christina of Sweden." She put the gold pound in her pocket and then watched the caravan leave. Olaf led the horse over and helped her mount. They walked slowly. After Christina had gone a distance, she reined in the horse. She sat on the horse and thought for a while, then looked at the road the caravan had taken. Suddenly, she turned the horse around and chased after the caravan.

Soon they had caught up with the caravan. She deliberately took off her hat and bowed deeply on horseback to the young man in the carriage. The man in the carriage returned the greeting in the same way. Christina laughed inwardly and hurried ahead. Olaf followed closely behind. As dusk approached, they arrived at an inn. She reined in the horse at the entrance, handed the horse to the inn's porter, and she and Olaf went into the inn. She entered the inn and looked around. There were several low wooden houses, lit by a few candles. In the fireplace, firewood was burning, emitting a blazing light. Many farming families were sitting around eating, and there were also a few soldiers pretending to be on duty. The porters were busy going back and forth with large trays. A large piece of meat was also roasting on the fire, which made Olaf's mouth water. Christina asked in a clear voice, "Where is the innkeeper?" A fat man ran up to her and asked, "What does the guest need?" Christina said, "Dinner, a room, a bed." The innkeeper sized her up and down and then said, "There is only one room left. It is the best room, specially for distinguished guests. The room fee is ten taels." Christina turned to Olaf and said, "Give him twenty taels!" The innkeeper, as if he had received a god of wealth, bowed deeply. While taking the money, he hurriedly led the way, repeatedly calling "Sir," and led them to a large room upstairs. Inside there was a large four-poster bed, a table, a mirror, and several chairs. In a large fireplace in the wall, wood had already been loaded, and it only needed a spark to ignite. Christina took off her hat and brushed off the snow. She felt very happy about this kind of naughty thing, like a mischievous child. Olaf was arranging the bedding in the room, and Christina went out to the corridor outside the room, looking down, eagerly hoping for the arrival of the Spanish caravan. (To be continued)
